# Connector Hub Engineering Trail Index - 2026-06-24

**Status:** Scenario-first engineering trail index for the current ConnectorHub local fixture proof package.
**Verdict:** `needs-follow-up` for the full ConnectorHub adoption goal; `PASS` is limited to the 40 AI-owned local proof rows listed below, while 7 rows remain `HUMAN_REQUIRED`.

## Scope Boundary

- This index is a discovery and audit map for ConnectorHub scenario-result artifacts.
- It does not claim live-provider readiness, human UX/privacy acceptance, physical-device behavior, production tenancy/RLS/OPA/egress readiness, backup/restore readiness, or release approval.
- `CS-CH-036` uses `local_vs2_topology`; all other AI-owned PASS rows use deterministic `local_fixture` proof.
- Human rows `CS-CH-H01` through `CS-CH-H07` remain `HUMAN_REQUIRED`; their templates and preparation report are evidence-preparation artifacts, not PASS evidence.
- Human-gate preparation is now guarded structurally: each template must name its scenario, preserve no-PASS/HUMAN_REQUIRED boundary language, include a scenario-first runbook or study script, include an Acceptance Evidence Packet with pending human-result rows, and name reject conditions. Each proposed reviewer-record template also includes a typed evidence-packet manifest skeleton with `required_evidence` labels and `allowed_redaction_statuses=redacted,public_safe,no_sensitive_material`, field-level `redaction_guidance`, `reviewer_checklist`, plus `record_template_output_command`, `validation_command`, and `validation_output_command`. Each package and rollup row also includes `scenario_delivery_unit_plan`, which maps senior-perspective research, implementation approach definition, smallest complete rehearsal, remediation/refactor, structural verification, result documentation, and dependency-aware next-gate movement while keeping product/PASS/approval flags false, plus `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_summary` so scripts can check `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_ready=true`, seven lifecycle steps, senior-review perspective count, and false product/PASS/approval/dependency-unlock plan flags without parsing the nested plan. `cornerstone connector human-gate package --scenario <id> --json --record-template-output <reviewer-record-template.json>` writes only the blank reviewer-record template; it is not approval or PASS evidence and remains intentionally invalid until completed by a human. The `reviewer_checklist` maps required fields, senior-review perspectives, evidence-packet rows, dependency refs, and validation commands while keeping product/PASS claims false. `cornerstone connector human-gate validate-record --json` requires complete manifest coverage, matching evidence labels, and allowed redaction statuses without persisting manifest values, also requires unique evidence refs, and returns `redaction_guidance` for safe reviewer correction. Duplicate evidence-packet refs are surfaced in validation-handoff issue summaries as `duplicate_evidence_packet_manifest_refs` with short SHA-256 fingerprints only; raw evidence refs remain omitted. `cornerstone connector human-gate validate-record --json --output <redacted-validation-envelope.json>` writes the same redacted structural-validation envelope with top-level `summary` and `final_verdict=HUMAN_REQUIRED`; it is not approval or PASS evidence. The `cornerstone connector human-gate report --json` output exposes the same readiness fields plus `summary.readiness_report_id`, manifest completion counts, `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_ready_count`, `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_missing=[]`, row-level `record_template_output_command`, row-level `record_validation_output_command`, and depends-on human-gate record validation readiness fields without changing any H row to `PASS`. Structurally valid `REJECT` records remain validation evidence but do not unlock dependent H gates. `cornerstone connector human-gate next --json` selects the first uncompleted dependency-ready H gate, lists blocked gates by missing dependency validation, exposes `next_record_template_output_command`, exposes `next_record_validation_output_command`, exposes `next_record_redaction_guidance`, exposes `next_reviewer_checklist`, exposes `next_scenario_delivery_unit_plan`, exposes `next_scenario_delivery_unit_plan_summary`, exposes `next_remaining_human_evidence_summary` with `claim_boundary=remaining_human_evidence_summary_is_operator_input_not_acceptance`, mirrors `next_scenario_delivery_unit_plan_ready`, active-gate command aliases, `next_remaining_human_evidence_summary`, remaining-evidence schema/required field names/evidence labels/redacted validation-output command, evidence-packet workflow schema/commands/no-acceptance flags, `next_required_human_delta`, and `readiness_report_ref` in top-level summary, and exposes H04-only local baseline comparison inputs when H04 is next. `cornerstone connector human-gate validation-handoff --json` compacts readiness into an ordered H-row validation handoff with validation status, dependency blockers, reviewer commands, latest validation refs and redacted latest-validation issue summaries when present, H04 local-baseline summary counts, row-level `remaining_human_evidence_summary` with `claim_boundary=remaining_human_evidence_summary_is_operator_input_not_acceptance`, summary-level `readiness_report_ref`, `blocked_dependency_details` for dependency-blocked rows, and zero approval/PASS/product-claim counters. Each human-gate package/report/next/validation-handoff/validate-record artifact and its top-level summary must expose `goal_completion_claim_blocked=true`, `full_goal_completion_allowed=false`, and `completion_claim_boundary=connectorhub_full_goal_requires_dated_accept_records_for_all_human_external_gates`; these fields make the full-goal completion block script-visible until all dated human/external accept records exist. Only structurally valid ACCEPT validation refs unlock dependent H gates.
- The human-gate next selector now also exposes active-gate validation correction metadata when a reviewer record exists: `next_record_validation_count`, `next_record_validation_status`, `next_latest_record_validation_ref`, `next_latest_record_validation_dependency_unlock_allowed`, and redacted `next_latest_record_validation_issue_summary`. This is operator correction metadata only; it cannot record a human decision, collect approval, or promote a H row to `PASS`.
- The next-selector top-level summary now mirrors active-gate redaction/checklist aliases: redaction schema/status, allowed redaction statuses, sensitive-marker policy schema and fingerprints-only flag, raw-secret/provider/evidence/body/path safety flags, required-field/evidence/dependency counts, checklist schema/status, checklist required-field/senior-review/evidence-manifest/dependency counts, checklist reviewer-record validation flag, checklist template and validation-output commands, checklist evidence-packet workflow command count/claim boundary, and checklist product/PASS claim flags. These aliases are operator scripting shortcuts only; they do not expose raw reviewer evidence, collect approval, or accept the gate.
- The validation-handoff row and top-level summary now mirror the same active-gate redaction/checklist aliases for the ordered H-row handoff. These aliases remain operator scripting shortcuts only; they do not expose raw reviewer evidence, collect approval, or accept the gate.

it writes `reports/scenario/connectorhub-human-gate-evidence-packet-file-contract-cs-ch-h04-2026-06-24.json` during artifact generation. `cornerstone connector human-gate preflight-bundle --scenario CS-CH-H04 --json` exposes the local comparison bundle as a first-class envelope with `schema_version=cs.connector_human_gate_preflight_bundle_report.v1`, `final_verdict=HUMAN_REQUIRED`, `goal_completion_claim_blocked=true`, `full_goal_completion_allowed=false`, `commands_executed_by_preflight_bundle=0`, `live_provider_calls_executed_by_preflight_bundle=0`, `provider_mutations_executed_by_preflight_bundle=0`, and `external_mutations_executed_by_preflight_bundle=0`; ## Human-Gate Preparation Guard

The seven H-row templates are ready for operator execution, not promotion. Each per-scenario package now carries the matching template path, structure readiness, review order, dependencies, gate category, stop/reject condition, a typed `scenario_delivery_unit_plan`, a typed `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_summary`, and a blank `proposed_record_template` JSON skeleton derived from the required human-record fields. The plan names seven lifecycle phases: senior-perspective research, implementation approach definition, smallest complete rehearsal, remediation/refactor, structural verification, result documentation, and dependency-aware next-gate movement. It keeps `product_claim_allowed_by_plan=false`, `pass_claim_allowed_by_plan=false`, `approval_collected_by_plan=false`, and `dependency_unlock_allowed_by_plan=false`; the summary mirrors those false flags with `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_ready=true`, seven lifecycle steps, and the senior-review perspective count for operator scripts. The skeleton is intentionally invalid until a human fills every required evidence field, every senior-review perspective finding, every typed evidence-packet manifest entry, and every dependency ref, and its `format_rules.review_timestamp` requires an ISO-8601 timestamp with timezone. Each manifest entry carries the expected `required_evidence` label and must use `redaction_status` `redacted`, `public_safe`, or `no_sensitive_material`. Each proposed template also carries `record_template_output_command`, so `cornerstone connector human-gate package --scenario <id> --json --record-template-output <reviewer-record-template.json>` can write only the blank reviewer-record template to a local file without extracting nested JSON by hand; that file is still preparation data, not approval evidence. Each proposed template also carries `reviewer_checklist`, so the same output tells operators which required fields, Senior Review Perspectives, evidence-packet rows, dependency refs, and validation command must be completed before submission. Each proposed template also carries `redaction_guidance` so operators can see that raw secrets, raw provider payloads, raw evidence values, raw record bodies, and raw record paths are disallowed, and that dependency refs must point at structurally valid ACCEPT `connector_human_gate_record_validation:<id>` artifacts. Each human template also carries a `Senior Review Perspectives` table, and the CLI readiness report exposes senior-review-perspective readiness through `senior_review_perspectives_ready_count` and row-level template-structure fields. Proposed human-review JSON can be checked with `cornerstone connector human-gate validate-record --scenario <id> --record-file <json> --json` or pinned with `cornerstone connector human-gate validate-record --scenario <id> --record-file <json> --json --output <redacted-validation-envelope.json>`; this validates required fields, decision values, senior-review perspective coverage, evidence-packet manifest coverage including label/status checks, dependency gate refs to existing structurally valid ACCEPT `connector_human_gate_record_validation:<id>` artifacts, timestamp format, and sensitive-marker findings without persisting the submitted record body, raw record path, decision value, senior-review finding text, or manifest values, while the output envelope mirrors top-level `summary` and `final_verdict=HUMAN_REQUIRED` without changing any H row out of `HUMAN_REQUIRED`. Structurally valid `REJECT` records remain validation evidence but do not unlock dependent H gates. The aggregate preparation report records the prepared operator script, evidence packet focus, explicit reject boundary, execution queue, existing record-validation coverage, blank record-template shape, scenario delivery-unit plan shape, scenario delivery-unit plan summary shape, reviewer checklist shape, senior-review-perspective readiness, evidence-packet manifest readiness, and depends-on human-gate record validation readiness fields for each H row, and the CLI readiness report exposes matching template-structure counters, `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_ready_count`, `scenario_delivery_unit_plan_missing=[]`, validation counts, senior-review finding completion counts, evidence-packet manifest completion counts, dependency readiness, dependency unlock counts, scenario order, top-level `summary`, top-level `final_verdict=HUMAN_REQUIRED`, and row-level `record_template_output_command`. `cornerstone connector human-gate next --json` selects the first uncompleted dependency-ready H gate, lists blocked gates by missing dependency validation, exposes `next_record_template_output_command`, exposes `next_record_validation_output_command`, exposes `next_reviewer_checklist`, exposes `next_scenario_delivery_unit_plan`, exposes `next_scenario_delivery_unit_plan_summary`, exposes `next_record_redaction_guidance`, mirrors `next_scenario_delivery_unit_plan_ready`, plan-step counts, active-gate command aliases, `next_remaining_human_evidence_summary`, `next_required_human_delta`, and `readiness_report_ref` into the summary, and when H04 is next, mirrors the local-baseline review inputs, required human delta, recommended preflight commands, and structured preflight command plan while preserving `acceptance_sufficient=false`. The verifier also fails if a human template regresses to a bare placeholder.

## Objective Completion Audit

This audit maps the active ConnectorHub goal to current repo evidence. It is intentionally stricter than the aggregate scenario verifier: a local fixture PASS does not prove live-provider, physical-device, human-acceptance, or production readiness.

Source objective clauses preserved by this audit:

- Validate and evolve ConnectorHub through a scenario-first process.
- Treat each `MUST_PASS` scenario as an independent delivery unit.
- Research from multiple senior developer perspectives before implementation.
- Define implementation approach, implement the smallest complete solution, then refactor/harden.
- Verify that each scenario passes before documenting it as complete.
- Document the result and explain how it contributes to ConnectorHub adoption in CornerStone.
- Preserve product value, domain correctness, architecture, data contracts, reliability, security, observability, performance, testability, maintainability, and migration feasibility.
- Final outcome is both working implementation and a clear engineering trail.

Summary counters: `objective_completion_audit_guarded=true`, `objective_completion_audit_count=7`, `objective_completion_audit_trace_ready_count=7`, `objective_completion_audit_local_ai_satisfied_count=5`, `objective_completion_audit_human_required_pending_count=1`, `objective_completion_audit_full_goal_not_complete_count=1`, `objective_completion_audit_goal_completion_claim_blocked_count=7`, `objective_completion_audit_full_goal_completion_allowed_count=0`, `objective_completion_audit_ids=independent_ai_delivery_units,senior_perspective_decision_research,implementation_refactor_verification_loop,connectorhub_adoption_trail,source_contract_alignment,human_external_proof_boundary,full_goal_completion_boundary`, and `objective_completion_audit_claim_boundary=objective_completion_audit_is_local_progress_not_full_goal_completion`.

|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

## Source Requirement Enrichment Overrides

| Scenario | Added requirements | Rationale | Source refs | Claim boundary |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `CS-CH-040` | `ER-07` | CS-CH-040 is the report-lint guard that keeps the ConnectorHub evidence package engineer-executable: it forces scenario reports to preserve row statuses, human-required gates, exact evidence, negative overclaim counters, and weakest-verdict boundaries instead of becoming a descriptive summary. | `Implementation document line 78`, `Implementation document line 159`, `Application guide lines 1506-1514`, `CS-CH-040 contract` | `requirement_enrichment_is_engineering_trail_scope_not_additional_runtime_proof` |

## Application Guide Adoption Conclusion Trace

The engineering-trail verifier validates `reports/scenario/connectorhub-scenario-delivery-unit-manifest-2026-06-24.json` against the current matrix, result docs, focused JSON reports, and focused gate output, requiring 40 closed AI delivery units, zero incomplete delivery units, 7 excluded human-required rows, exact closed AI and excluded human scenario ID sets, exact focused verify/gate commands for each delivery unit, focused gate status `success`, focused gate scenario count `1`, zero focused gate blocking rows, zero focused gate errors, parsed source requirement IDs, a machine-readable source-requirement proof split with 16 AI-only requirements, 11 human-pending requirements, zero requirements without AI delivery-unit coverage, 17 human-required source-requirement links, and the claim boundary `ai_local_coverage_does_not_close_human_external_slices`, machine-readable present/missing coverage for all eleven decision dimensions, all five research perspective families, and all lifecycle markers, complete decision/lifecycle/research/implementation/refactor/verification/documentation/adoption closure flags, focused report facts, local proof boundary, and false product/live/human/production claim flags. It validates `reports/scenario/connectorhub-engineering-trail-manifest-2026-06-24.json` against the current file bytes for the contract, matrix, index, verifier, manifest generator, Makefile, root `cornerstone` CLI launcher, Connector runtime, CLI entrypoint, focused ConnectorHub CLI tests, README, 40 AI result docs, 40 AI JSON evidence reports, 7 human templates, pinned human package JSONs, pinned H04 field-ref-contract JSON, pinned all-H evidence-packet-contract JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-file-contract JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-scaffold JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-validation JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-record-draft JSONs, pinned H04 preflight-bundle JSON, pinned human readiness JSON, pinned human next-selector JSON, pinned human validation-handoff JSON, pinned blank reviewer-record templates for all seven H rows, pinned blank-template blocked validation envelopes for all seven H rows, aggregate report, human preparation report, and scenario delivery-unit manifest. It also validates the Makefile target entry points for `verify-connector-contract-adapter`, `verify-connectorhub-engineering-trail`, `generate-connectorhub-human-gate-artifacts`, and `generate-connectorhub-engineering-trail-manifest`, so the documented make commands refresh the current VS2 local proof and VS2 scenario report before focused ConnectorHub replay, replay the exact 40 matrix-backed AI focused verify/gate pairs, refresh pinned human-gate artifacts including `reports/scenario/connectorhub-human-gate-field-ref-contract-cs-ch-h04-2026-06-24.json`, all-H evidence-packet contract/file-contract/scaffold/validation/record-draft JSON report sets, and `reports/scenario/connectorhub-human-gate-preflight-bundle-cs-ch-h04-2026-06-24.json`, generate all seven blank reviewer-record templates, validate each blank template into a blocked redacted envelope, then call the expected verifier and manifest-generator scripts. It validates that the manifest generator imports the verifier, builds the scenario delivery-unit manifest, reuses `_required_manifest_paths(rows)` and `SOURCE_INPUTS`, preserves source-only external input boundaries, keeps the local-fixture/local-VS2 claim boundary, and writes `verdict=needs-follow-up`. It validates the matrix ledger shape: exact columns, unique scenario IDs, expected `CS-CH-001` through `CS-CH-040` plus `CS-CH-H01` through `CS-CH-H07`, expected type/owner/status counts, non-empty row fields, and AI/Human proof-surface boundaries. The artifact set must be exact: stale or extra ConnectorHub result docs, focused scenario reports, human templates, pinned human package JSONs, pinned H04 field-ref-contract JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-contract JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-file-contract JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-scaffold JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-validation JSONs, pinned all-H evidence-packet-record-draft JSONs, pinned H04 preflight-bundle JSONs, pinned human next-selector JSONs, pinned human validation-handoff JSONs, pinned H-row record-template JSONs, pinned H-row blank-validation JSONs, aggregate reports, scenario delivery-unit manifests, or engineering-trail manifests fail the verifier even if the matrix itself is clean. The canonical contract Proof Surface Matrix must preserve UI/API as `NOT_VERIFIED`, human gates/live provider/production as `HUMAN_REQUIRED`, and the done-criteria boundary-discipline sentence before the index or manifest can pass. The canonical contract Engineering Trail Maintenance section must also preserve its independent scenario delivery loop, package refresh sequence, focused-report done criteria, scenario delivery-unit manifest boundary, and manifest-refresh boundary before any future scenario PASS claim. The canonical contract Scenario Result Policy proof-command block must exactly match the 40 AI-owned matrix `evidence_required` paths plus the aggregate command and must not include `CS-CH-H01` through `CS-CH-H07`. The Source Requirement Coverage table must exactly match the ER/IR-to-scenario mapping derived from `docs/scenario-contracts/CONNECTOR_HUB_APPLICATION_MATRIX.csv`. The Proof Surface Summary and Phase Summary tables must also match matrix-derived proof-surface counts, claim-boundary labels, and AI-owned PASS row phase counts. The AI-Owned Scenario Trail and Human-Required Gate Trail tables must exactly match matrix-derived row content, not just contain matching tokens elsewhere in the index. The Verification Commands list must remain the exact ordered set shown above, so the trail cannot drift away from the verifier, manifest generation, human-gate artifact replay, all-H blank-template artifact replay, compile, SoT-doc, CLI-native-first-doc, and scenario-matrix checks used for this package. The Independent Delivery Unit Rule must also preserve the ordered freeze, research, implement/refactor, focused-report gate, result-documentation, scenario delivery-unit manifest refresh, pinned human-gate package/field-ref-contract/evidence-packet-contract/evidence-packet-file-contract/evidence-packet-scaffold/preflight-bundle/readiness/next-selector/validation-handoff artifact refresh, and engineering-trail manifest refresh loop before future scenario PASS claims. The Remaining Proof Surfaces section must preserve the exact unresolved human/external blocker list, including the H-row boundaries for live GitHub, physical macOS capture, Chrome privacy, production topology/recovery, live non-GitHub Action, and usability/trust acceptance. The aggregate report must contain exactly the sorted AI-owned PASS matrix IDs, must exclude human-required rows, and must keep each aggregate row's owner, type, status, evidence, and notes intact. Aggregate and focused JSON reports must preserve the `cs.cli.v0` report envelope, CornerStone product identity, local scope identity, command transcript, shared `ids.git_commit`, matching absolute `output_path`, and matching transcript `--output` artifact path. Each focused AI JSON report must also contain exactly one `scenario_results` row matching the matrix scenario ID, type, owner, and PASS status, with non-empty evidence entries and notes as the focused acceptance record. Focused evidence command coverage is also guarded: concrete `cornerstone ... --json` evidence commands in focused AI reports must map to captured CLI transcripts with valid `cs.cli.v0` JSON, template commands must stay explicit CLI-shaped entries, and reusable VS2 proof commands must cite existing report artifacts. The CS-CH-036 raw unittest replay guard requires `tests/scenario/test_connectorhub_cli.py` to refresh `reports/security/vs2-local-security-proof.json` and `reports/scenario/vs2-policy-tenancy-egress-2026-06-19.json` before direct CS-CH-036 default-deny assertions, so filtered unittest replay cannot consume stale VS2 fingerprint evidence.

CLI scenario registry coverage is guarded through both public aliases: `connectorhub` and `connector-contract-adapter` must return exactly the 47 canonical matrix rows, including titles, owners, scenario types, expected results, verification methods, and the human-required gate IDs.

When any listed artifact or source input changes, regenerate the pinned human-gate package/field-ref-contract/evidence-packet-contract/evidence-packet-file-contract/evidence-packet-scaffold/evidence-packet-validation/evidence-packet-record-draft/preflight-bundle/readiness/next/validation-handoff artifacts, scenario delivery-unit manifest, and engineering-trail manifest with `make generate-connectorhub-engineering-trail-manifest`, then run `make verify-connectorhub-engineering-trail`. The generator imports the verifier's manifest path list and source input list so the hash set has one maintained source of truth.

## Independent Delivery Unit Rule

For future ConnectorHub evolution, each `MUST_PASS` row must close as one scenario-delivery unit before the next scenario receives a PASS claim:

1. Freeze the row's scenario id, related requirements, proof surface, claim boundary, focused CLI verifier command, and evidence report path.
2. Research the five perspective families captured in each result doc: product/domain, architecture/data-contract, reliability/security, observability/performance/testability, and maintainability/migration.
3. Implement the smallest complete behavior and refactor inside that scenario's dependency boundary.
4. Regenerate the focused JSON evidence report and gate it before updating the aggregate.
5. Document the scenario result with decision trail, lifecycle trail, negative evidence, proof boundary, and ConnectorHub adoption contribution.
6. Regenerate the pinned human-gate package/field-ref-contract/evidence-packet-contract/evidence-packet-file-contract/evidence-packet-scaffold/evidence-packet-validation/evidence-packet-record-draft/preflight-bundle/readiness/next-selector/validation-handoff artifacts, scenario delivery-unit manifest, and engineering-trail manifest, then rerun `make verify-connectorhub-engineering-trail`.

The focused JSON evidence report and result document are the scenario's acceptance record. The aggregate report and this index are rollups; they cannot replace the focused proof.

## Remaining Proof Surfaces

Summary counters: `remaining_proof_surface_guarded=true`, `remaining_proof_surface_count=7`, `remaining_proof_surface_ids=CS-CH-H04,CS-CH-H07,CS-CH-H01,CS-CH-H02,CS-CH-H03,CS-CH-H05,CS-CH-H06`, `remaining_proof_surface_trace_ready_count=7`, `remaining_proof_surface_next_count=1`, `remaining_proof_surface_next_scenario_ids=CS-CH-H04`, `remaining_proof_surface_dependency_ready_count=1`, `remaining_proof_surface_dependency_ready_ids=CS-CH-H04`, `remaining_proof_surface_dependency_blocked_count=6`, `remaining_proof_surface_dependency_blocked_ids=CS-CH-H07,CS-CH-H01,CS-CH-H02,CS-CH-H03,CS-CH-H05,CS-CH-H06`, `remaining_proof_surface_remaining_field_total=72`, `remaining_proof_surface_remaining_evidence_total=29`, `remaining_proof_surface_completion_allowed_count=0`, `remaining_proof_surface_pass_claim_allowed_count=0`, `remaining_proof_surface_product_claim_allowed_count=0`, and `remaining_proof_surface_claim_boundary=remaining_human_external_gate_audit_is_operator_handoff_not_human_acceptance`.

- The human execution order, stop conditions, and promotion rule are defined in `docs/verification-reports/CONNECTOR_HUB_HUMAN_GATES_PREPARATION_REPORT_2026-06-24.md`.
- Live GitHub read-only readiness remains blocked by `CS-CH-H01`.
- Physical macOS capture behavior remains blocked by `CS-CH-H02`.
- Real Chrome privacy/permission acceptance remains blocked by `CS-CH-H03`.
- Production-like RequestContext, PostgreSQL/RLS, OPA, egress, backup/restore, and audit readiness remain blocked by `CS-CH-H04` and `CS-CH-H07`.
- Live side-effecting non-GitHub Action readiness remains blocked by `CS-CH-H05`.
- Human usability/trust acceptance remains blocked by `CS-CH-H06`.
